commit d9de194cbca1a945720a012966a7750316536d88
Author: Kenny Root <kenny@the-b.org>
Date:   Wed Oct 23 20:03:49 2013 -0700

    Use KeyId instead of NId for TNEANet attributes
    
    Add{Int,Str,Flt}AttrDat[NE] use the NodeH.GetKeyId(NId) and
    EdgeH.GetKeyId(EId) for their index into the attribute vectors, but the
    rest of the functions did not. This would allow the functions to still
    work if all the nodes corresponded exactly between the NId and the
    KeyId, but this doesn't happen when you use LoadEdgeList.

 1 file changed, 24 insertions(+), 24 deletions(-)

commit 0728ee3f81d225b59b717719bb6c8a0efa53c6f0
Author: Rok Sosic <rok@cs.stanford.edu>
Date:   Wed Aug 8 17:27:12 2012 -0700

    make the behavior of AddNode() and AddEdge() consistent across graphs and networks
    
    AddNode()
            creates a new node, if NId = -1
            returns NId, if a node is added
            aborts, if NId exists
    AddEdge() for single graphs
            returns -2, set edge data (for networks), if an edge exits
            returns -1, if a new edge is added
    AddEdge() for multi graphs
            returns EId, if an edge is added
            aborts, if EId exists
